USA beat Armenia 1-0 FULLERTON, California, May 15 (AFP) -The United States beat Armenia 1-0 in a friendly international football match here Sunday. The US team posted their fourth victory of the year as they prepare to host the 1994 World Cup finals June 17-July 17. For the first two thirds of the match, Armenia's defense stymied the United States. But the Americans profited from a let-down by the visitors and had several scoring opportunities in the closing stages. Frank Klopas scored on a counter attack, firing an angled shot from 25 meters that hit the right upright and went in. Scorers USA 1 (Klopas 64), Armenia 0 bb94

(correcting ex-NICOSIA) In Iraq-Saddam,2ndlead, eleventh para, please read it x x x Ramadan had been since March 22, 1991 one of the country's two vice presidents, along with Taha Mohieddin Maaruf, a Kurd who was appointed on April 24, 1974. Maaruf is considered as a renegade by Kurdish nationalists who control the Kurdistan region of northern Iraq, which has enjoyed de facto autonomy since rebelling against Baghdad at the end of the Gulf war in 1991. The nomination of a Kurd to the post of vice president is called for under Iraq's "provisional" constitution.
